Set the cost per hour for a resource and the time a resource spent working on a task. Based on these figures, GanttPRO will instantly calculate task, group of task and project costs. Too expensive? Our project planning app allows you to reallocate resources and see how the expenses change.</p>\n        </div>\n      </section>\n    </div>\n\n  </article>\n  <!-- /sides-preview -->\n\n  <!-- software-feat -->\n  <article class=\"software-feat bg-white\">\n    <div class=\"global-container\">\n\n      <div class=\"feat_head\">\n        <h2 class=\"head_title\">Features of GanttPRO. From a simple Gantt chart to complex project management.</h2>\n        \n      </div>\n\n      <div class=\"feat_slider\">\n        <div class=\"slider_menu\">\n          <div class=\"menu_list js-menu-list\">\n            <a class=\"list_item active\" data-next=\"view-1\">Custom working days and hours</a>\n            <a class=\"list_item\" data-next=\"view-2\">Real time notifications</a>\n            <a class=\"list_item\" data-next=\"view-3\">Critical path on Gantt chart</a>\n            <a class=\"list_item\" data-next=\"view-4\">Comments and attachments</a>\n            <a class=\"list_item\" data-next=\"view-5\">Export Gantt chart to popular formats</a>\n            <a class=\"list_item\" data-next=\"view-6\">Save projects as templates</a>\n            <a class=\"list_item\" data-next=\"view-7\">Gantt chart dependencies</a>\n            <a class=\"list_item\" data-next=\"view-8\">Gantt chart milestones</a>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"slider_view\">\n          <div class=\"view_section js-view-section active\" style=\"height: 597.75px;\">\n\n            <div class=\"section_item active\" id=\"view-1\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/custom.png\" alt=\"Custom working days and hours\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Custom working days and hours</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">Plan your projects with custom working hours and days! GanttPRO will calculate the duration of your Gantt chart projects automatically based on peculiarities of your working days during the week.\n</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"section_item\" id=\"view-2\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/noti.png\" alt=\"Real time notifications\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Real time notifications</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">Be on top of the latest changes in all your shared Gantt charts! Collaborate with your team members and catch up with new comments quickly and see who has granted you or changed project rights.<br><br>Track all changes in team roles and rights and see who uses the online timeline maker now.</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"section_item\" id=\"view-3\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/path.png\" alt=\"Critical path on Gantt chart\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Critical path on Gantt chart</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">Enable a critical path on your Gantt chart to see a chain of tasks that affects the whole project duration.<br><br>With a critical path on your Gantt chart, you are always able to see the shortest time in which a project can be completed and tasks to which you should pay attention.</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"section_item\" id=\"view-4\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/com.png\" alt=\"Comments and attachments\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Comments and attachments</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">Leave comments for your team members on tasks our use Gantt chart software as a file storage. Easily attach files and share them with team members and clients. You won't miss a thing as we send instant notifications about chat or storage updates.\n</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"section_item\" id=\"view-5\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/export.png\" alt=\"Export Gantt chart to popular formats\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Export Gantt chart to popular formats</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">Create and share your Gantt diagram! Provide your clients with activity duration estimates or show a project’s progress. Visualize your project plans and make them work for you!<br><br>Easily export Gantt charts to XLSX, PNG, PDF or iCal. Share project plans using links or send them via email, giving the right to edit or the right to view your charts.</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"section_item\" id=\"view-6\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/templates.png\" alt=\"Save projects as templates\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Save projects as templates</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">GanttPRO allows you to plan each project from scratch or use your saved project template.<br><br>You can also choose one of <a href=\"/gantt-chart-template/\">free Gantt chart templates</a>: from a simple project plan template to a software development project plan template, a construction schedule template, a web design project plan template and many other.</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"section_item\" id=\"view-7\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/dependencies.png\" alt=\"Gantt chart dependencies\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Gantt chart dependencies</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">Connect tasks on your Gantt chart with dependencies. This helps our <a href=\"/gantt_scheduling/\">project scheduling software</a> allocate them automatically and create a project plan without your direct participation on setting start and end dates.<br><br>Using Gantt chart dependencies is the best way to manage a project plan. If one of the connected tasks is overdue, all the following tasks will be pushed forward accordingly.</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div class=\"section_item\" id=\"view-8\">\n              <div class=\"item_inner\">\n                <div class=\"inner_image\">\n                  <img class=\"image_img\" src=\"/media/images/software-feat/milestone.png\" alt=\"Gantt chart milestones\">\n                </div>\n                <h3 class=\"inner_title\">Gantt chart milestones</h3>\n                <p class=\"inner_txt\">In our Gantt chart creator, in order to mark an achievement or any other important point, you can use milestones.<br><br>When connecting Gantt bars with a milestone chart in software project management or any other, you and your team always see important dates. A Gantt chart milestone has the same scheduling features as a Gantt bar. If a project is rescheduled, your milestones will be rescheduled as well.</p>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      <div class=\"feat_navigate\">\n        <div class=\"navigate_left js-navigate-left\">←</div>\n        <div class=\"navigate_right js-navigate-right\">→</div>\n      </div>\n\n    </div>\n  </article>\n  <!-- /software-feat -->\n\n  <!-- client-feedback -->\n  <article class=\"client-feedback bg-noise\">\n    <div class=\"global-container\">\n\n      <h2 class=\"feedback_title\">Our clients suggest GanttPRO to their colleagues and partners</h2>\n\n      <div class=\"feedback_quotes\">\n        <svg class=\"quotes_svg\" viewBox=\"0 0 46 28\" style=\"width:4.6rem;height:2.8rem;\">\n          <use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"#icon_quotes_big\"></use>\n        </svg>\n      </div>\n\n      <div class=\"feedback_text js-feedback-text\" style=\"height: 72px;\">\n        <div class=\"text_item\" id=\"client-feedback-1\">\n          How incredibly powerful this cloud-based Gantt planner can be! <span class=\"yellow-highlight\">It is well priced considering the powerful interface.
